"integumentary tissue-trunk torso, anterior posterior, external approach. this class includes one or more of 20 standard surgical interventions or procedures on component parts of the integumentary tissue of anterior and posterior trunk and torso with external approach.  these surgical interventions or procedures are listed in the world health organizations international statistical classification of diseases and related health problems or icd-10 pcs under code 0h.. transfer buttock skin,  external approach. this classification denotes the group of activities that yields a surgical intervention or procedure to transfer buttock skin,  external approach.this surgical intervention or procedure is listed in the world health organizations international statistical classification of diseases and related health problems or icd-10 as code 0hx8xzz. "
